    SELECT v."VendorId", v."ApprovalStatusId", v."CompanyEmail", v."CompanyPhoneNumber", v."ContactPersonName", v."CreatedAt", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."ReviewedAt", v."ReviewedByAdminId", v."VendorCompanyName"
